</th>

<div class="we"><div id="IMSLP190951" class="we_file_first we_fileblock_9">

<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Peer Gynt Suite No.1
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Grieg,_Edvard" title="Category:Grieg, Edvard">Grieg, Edvard</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>Op.46
</td></tr>

</th>
<td>IEG 77
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>4 movements:
<dl><dd>1. Morning Mood
</dd><dd>2. Death of Åse
</dd><dd>3. Anitra's Dance
</dd><dd>4. In the Hall of the Mountain King
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
<tr>

</th>
<td>1888
</td></tr>

</td></tr>

</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Instrumentation
</th>
<td><i>Orchestra:</i> piccolo, 2 flutes, 2 oboes, 2 clarinets, 2 bassoons<br />4 horns, 2 trumpets, 3 trombones, tuba<br />timpani, cymbals, bass drum, triangle, strings
